| 0:05:05| which any liquor other than beer is covered under the Alcoholic Beverage Administration of the State of Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=305)|
| 0:05:13| Commission Administration, ABC.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=313)|

| 0:06:23| ABC has authority to jerk their liquor license altogether.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=383)|
| 0:06:27| We can't jerk their beer license because the way I read the law right now,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=387)|
| 0:06:34| until the legislature wants to change it, sale of a slushie or whatever they call those things now, seems to be in the gray area.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=394)|

| 1:04:24| Our particular office is very fortunate to be funded both by the state and the county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3864)|
| 1:04:30| You provide about 40 percent of our budget every year. We're 60 percent state funded, about 40 percent county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3870)|

| 1:04:49| because you actually have the year-end review with you.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3889)|
| 1:04:52| But just so you'll know, our office right now has 82 employees.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3892)|
| 1:04:57| Forty-two of those are assistant district attorneys. The other 40 are support staff.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3897)|

| 1:05:10| and that staff also is split about 60-40 state, county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3910)|
| 1:05:14| As you look through the year-end report, you'll notice that there's a lot of information about units in our office,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3914)|
| 1:05:20| and I wanted to take just a minute to explain to you what a unit is.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3920)|
| 1:05:24| With those 42 assistant district attorneys, instead of letting each of those assistant district attorneys| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3924)|
| 1:05:30| prosecute all different types of crime, we have divided the office so that we have, if you will,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3930)|
| 1:05:37| little mini law offices within our office.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3937)|
| 1:05:40| Each little mini unit specializes on a particular type of crime,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3940)|
| 1:05:45| the theory being that if a unit prosecutes the same type of crime all the time and is trained in that,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3945)|
| 1:05:51| they will be better prepared to actually address that particular type of crime.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3951)|
| 1:05:56| We have eight specialized units in our office.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3956)|
| 1:05:59| For example, we have a child abuse unit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3959)|
| 1:06:02| They prosecute nothing but child sexual and physical abusers.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3962)|
| 1:06:06| There are four lawyers in that unit, and just to give you an idea,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3966)|
| 1:06:11| we prosecute way more sexual abuse crime in Knox County than we do physical abuse crime.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3971)|
| 1:06:17| We also have an elder abuse unit where the prosecutors and victim witness coordinators in that unit| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3977)|
| 1:06:23| focus on nothing but crimes involving persons over 65 years of age.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3983)|
| 1:06:28| I'm very proud to tell you that Knox County has the very first elder abuse unit in the state of Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3988)|
| 1:06:34| We created that when I took office back in 2014.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3994)|
| 1:06:37| It is a sad fact that in 2014 there was no district attorney's office in the entire state focusing on elder abuse,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=3997)|
| 1:06:44| but we have since remedied that.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4004)|
| 1:06:46| Since we began our unit in 2014,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4006)|
| 1:06:49| most other district attorney's offices around the state have now used our program as a model,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4009)|
| 1:06:54| and we have elder abuse units in most all prosecutor's offices throughout the state now.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4014)|
| 1:06:59| We have a domestic violence unit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4019)|
| 1:07:02| Every single year our domestic violence unit has more cases than any other unit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4022)|
| 1:07:07| In Knox County you're averaging about 1,700 domestic violence prosecutions per year.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4027)|
| 1:07:15| That is definitely the busiest unit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4035)|
| 1:07:17| You will see that as you look through the packet.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4037)|
| 1:07:19| We have a major crimes unit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4039)|
| 1:07:21| Our major crimes unit handles, as the name says, our most major crimes, which are homicides, rapes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4041)|

| 1:16:29| A couple of years ago, what we did here in this community was launch something called a pretrial risk assessment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4589)|
| 1:16:37| That is a tool that we came up with, I think it's been two years now,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4597)|
| 1:16:41| that now everyone that comes through Knox County and is booked has a pretrial risk assessment done on them| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4601)|
| 1:16:48| to determine what level basically of threat they are to the community, what their bond should be set at.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4608)|
| 1:16:56| That pretrial risk assessment has caused our pretrial numbers,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4616)|
| 1:17:00| people that are actually placed on pretrial release or ROR.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4620)|
| 1:17:04| ROR means release on your own recognizance.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4624)|
| 1:17:08| Those numbers have gone up significantly, meaning that fewer and fewer people who are charged with a crime| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4628)|
| 1:17:13| are actually being housed in our jail right now.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4633)|
| 1:17:16| That kind of goes hand in hand with an order that all eight of our judges,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4636)|
| 1:17:22| our three criminal court judges and our five sessions judges, have had a pretrial order in place throughout COVID.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4642)|
| 1:17:30| That order mandates that all people that are brought into custody with a misdemeanor charge or an E, D, or C felony| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4650)|
| 1:17:40| are to be looked at first for an ROR, a release on their own recognizance,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4660)|
| 1:17:46| followed by a pretrial, being placed on pretrial.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4666)|
| 1:17:49| Because of those orders, our jail numbers are down significantly.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4669)|
| 1:17:53| They are starting to creep back up as we start to run courts and people don't show up to court.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4673)|
| 1:17:59| Those numbers are creeping back up.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4679)|
| 1:18:01| But our jail numbers have been down significantly based on that pretrial risk assessment,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=4681)|

| 2:12:25| As I indicated, the staff's recommendation was based upon the application of the growth policy plan,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7945)|
| 2:12:30| and after staff provided this recommendation, the applicant hired me to look into that matter.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7950)|
| 2:12:37| And I wish I'd looked into this issue before because it actually surprised me in what I found.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7957)|
| 2:12:42| I first went to this body's resolution in 2019 where it voted to reinstate the growth policy plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7962)|
| 2:12:54| And in that resolution, the resolution specifically had a finding of fact that the growth policy plan,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7974)|
| 2:12:59| which was passed initially in 2001, had expired on its own terms at the end of 2007.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7979)|
| 2:13:06| And I didn't know why it stated that, so I started digging a little deeper.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7986)|
| 2:13:09| I reached out to the law director, David Boock, and asked him about that statement,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7989)|
| 2:13:14| and he provided an e-mail, which is in the record in the letter that I presented to planning commission on June 7.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=7994)|
| 2:13:20| He stated that it is the law director's opinion that the growth policy plan is no longer in force or effect| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8000)|
| 2:13:25| because it expired under its own terms.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8005)|
| 2:13:27| So I went deeper.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8007)|
| 2:13:28| I found a memo that the former law director, Bud Armstrong, had drafted where he reached the same conclusion,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8008)|
| 2:13:34| and he referred back to the original resolution that was adopted by the county commission in 2001.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8014)|
| 2:13:41| So I found that resolution, and sure enough, that resolution, all this is in the record attached to my letters,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8021)|
| 2:13:46| that resolution said that the growth policy plan shall expire on its own terms at the end of 2007,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8026)|
| 2:13:54| which goes back to why this body said to reapply and reinstate the growth policy plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8034)|
| 2:13:59| Now, that hasn't happened yet.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8039)|
| 2:14:01| This body passed it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8041)|
| 2:14:02| The city of Knoxville passed it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8042)|
| 2:14:04| Farragut blocked it, and so there's some still work to be done on what to do with the growth policy plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8044)|
| 2:14:09| But the resolution this body passed is also interesting as it relates to this issue today| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8049)|
| 2:14:14| in that the resolution passed by this body eliminated sections 3.2 to 3.6 of the growth policy plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8054)|
| 2:14:21| You guys will probably remember this conversation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8061)|
| 2:14:23| That is the part that talked about the limitations of extending densities greater than two dwelling units an acre| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8063)|
| 2:14:31| and up to three dwelling units an acre into the rural area of the growth policy plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8071)|
| 2:14:34| And what this body says, we shall let the sector plans decide.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8074)|
| 2:14:38| The sector plan in this case is low-density residential.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8078)|
| 2:14:42| Low-density residential in the county allows up to five dwelling units an acre, which is what the applicant asked for.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8082)|
| 2:14:48| So I presented that to the planning commission.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8088)|
| 2:14:51| The planning commission then split the baby and decided to give us four dwelling units an acre.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8091)|
| 2:14:56| And we are still here today asking for five dwelling units an acre, and I want to talk about that a little bit more.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8096)|
| 2:15:01| This piece of property is relatively unique in Knox County.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8101)|
| 2:15:04| It's 8.7 acres, but it's not any hillside protection.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8104)|
| 2:15:08| It's flat.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8108)|
| 2:15:09| It's accessed by Old Tazewell Pike and Murphy Road.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8109)|
| 2:15:15| Old Tazewell Pike is a local road, but Murphy Road is a major collector with 34.1 feet of pavement and a 70-foot right-of-way.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8115)|
| 2:15:22| There's no question there's sewer.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8122)|
| 2:15:24| There's infrastructure.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8124)|
| 2:15:25| There's no question that this property can handle the infrastructure required for the density of five dwelling units an acre.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8125)|
| 2:15:32| If you look back at the growth policy plan, this property is also unique,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8132)|
| 2:15:37| and immediately west of this property, across from Murphy Road, you're in the urban growth area.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8137)|
| 2:15:44| Right across this property, you're in the rural area.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8144)|
| 2:15:48| To the north, just a little ways above Old Tazewell, you're again in the urban growth area.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8148)|
| 2:15:52| Now, the growth policy plan provided in the past that it should be reviewed every three years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8152)|
| 2:15:57| to determine if there needs to be an extension or a change of the categories of these planned growth areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8157)|
| 2:16:04| And you have to think that never happened over 20 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8164)|
| 2:16:07| And you'd have to think this piece of property, surrounded by urban growth,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8167)|
| 2:16:11| would have at least been applied at a planned growth area, if not an urban growth area, over the last 20 years, had anybody reviewed it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8171)|
| 2:16:19| So, again, that also goes to supporting five dwelling units an acre.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8179)|
| 2:16:23| And why is five dwelling units an acre important in this case?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8183)|
| 2:16:27| It's only nine units when you look at the property itself, but that's nine units that this county desperately needs.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8187)|
| 2:16:33| It's been well documented that we are in a housing crisis, that we can't build them fast enough,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8193)|
| 2:16:38| that the costs of construction are skyrocketing, and we need affordable housing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8198)|
| 2:16:42| The plan for this property is to do attached units, which is a mixture of housing for seniors and housing for young families.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8202)|
| 2:16:51| And the intent is to do it in a way that it is in that affordable range, and I laid out all that in my letter.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8211)|
| 2:16:57| And in order to make that happen, you have to have economy of scale.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8217)|
| 2:17:02| You have to deal with the infrastructure costs, the construction costs,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8222)|
| 2:17:06| and being able to do more of that at one time will help offset those costs to help allow a product to be affordable.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8226)|
| 2:17:14| And we have also an urban sprawl problem, and this will also help solve that,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8234)|
| 2:17:18| because if we don't, if we lose nine units here,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8238)|
| 2:17:21| we're going to be looking at some other farm further in the rural area to try to make up those units| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8241)|
| 2:17:25| to meet the 40,000 plus demand that has been documented that we need in this county over the next few years,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8245)|
| 2:17:32| and that has, I think, been underreported.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210726-combined?start=8252)|
